The `number of followers` of users in Iraq on `2023/8/12 12:29 AM UTC`. This list contains users from `Iraq` and cities `Baghdad` `Mosul` `Basra` `Erbil` `Najaf`.

There are `138 countries` and `674 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/gayanvoice/top-github-users).

There are `946 users`  in Iraq. You need at least `3 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
